## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="cda0a-1827">Atributos de Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cda0a-1827">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cda0a-1828">Esta clase contiene los siguientes atributos para Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cda0a-1828">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
